margin-bottom: 30px; width: 100%; max-width: 100%; text-align: center;\">\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t<div style=\"width: 100%;\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div style=\"display: block; background: url('https://www.isnare.com/img/line-wide.png') repeat-x center center; text-align: center; margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 5px;\"><h1 style=\"text-align: center; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 34px !important; font-weight: 400 !important; color: #c9c9c0; text-shadow: 1px 1px 0px #fff; font-family: Georgia, Palatino, Palatino Linotype, Times, Times New Roman, serif !important;\">Encyclopedia</h1></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<center>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div style=\"text-align: left; padding-top: 20px; max-width: 88% !important; text-overflow: none; word-wrap: break-word; overflow: none;\"><div id=\"encycdivinner\" class=\"text\"><div id=\"mp-tfa-img\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.5em 0.9em 0.4em 0em;\"><a style=\"text-decoration: underline;\" rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"//www.isnare.com/encyclopedia/File:Shakespeare.jpg\" class=\"image\" title=\"The Chandos portrait, thought to depict Shakespeare\"><img style=\"border: 0px; border: 1px solid #AAA; -webkit-border-radius: 2px; border-radius: 2px; -webkit-box-shadow: 2px 3px 3px #DDD; box-shadow: 2px 3px 3px #DDD; background-color: #F9F9F9; background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #EEE, #F9F9F9, #EEE); background-image: linear-gradient(top, #EEE, #F9F9F9, #EEE);\" alt=\"The Chandos portrait, thought to depict Shakespeare\" src=\"//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Shakespeare.jpg/100px-Shakespeare.jpg\" width=\"100\" height=\"128\" srcset=\"//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Shakespeare.jpg/150px-Shakespeare.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Shakespeare.jpg/200px-Shakespeare.jpg 2x\" data-file-width=\"1943\" data-file-height=\"2489\"></a></div>\nThe <b><a style=\"text-decoration: underline;\" rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"//www.isnare.com/encyclopedia/Shakespeare_authorship_question\" title=\"Shakespeare authorship question\">Shakespeare authorship question</a></b> is the argument, first raised in the 19th century, that someone other than <a style=\"text-decoration: underline;\" rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"//www.isnare.com/encyclopedia/William_Shakespeare\" title=\"William Shakespeare\">William Shakespeare</a> of <a style=\"text-decoration: underline;\" rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"//www.isnare.com/encyclopedia/Stratford-upon-Avon\" title=\"Stratford-upon-Avon\">Stratford-upon-Avon</a> wrote the works attributed to him. All but a few Shakespeare scholars and literary historians consider it a <a style=\"text-decoration: underline;\" rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"//www.isnare.com/encyclopedia/Fringe_theory\" title=\"Fringe theory\">fringe belief</a>. Anti-Stratfordians believe that Shakespeare was a front to shield the identity of the real author or authors, who for some reason did not want or could not accept public credit. The controversy has spawned a vast body of literature, and <a style=\"text-decoration: underline;\" rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"//www.isnare.com/encyclopedia/List_of_Shakespeare_authorship_candidates\" title=\"List of Shakespeare authorship candidates\">more than 80 authorship candidates</a> have been proposed, the most popular being <a style=\"text-decoration: underline;\" rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"//www.isnare.com/encyclopedia/Francis_Bacon\" title=\"Francis Bacon\">Francis Bacon</a>, <a style=\"text-decoration: underline;\" rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"//www.isnare.com/encyclopedia/Edward_de_Vere\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"Edward de Vere\">Edward de Vere</a>, <a style=\"text-decoration: underline;\" rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"//www.isnare.com/encyclopedia/Christopher_Marlowe\" title=\"Christopher Marlowe\">Christopher Marlowe</a>, and <a style=\"text-decoration: underline;\" rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"//www.isnare.com/encyclopedia/William_Stanley,_6th_Earl_of_Derby\" title=\"William Stanley, 6th Earl of Derby\">William Stanley</a>. To the claim that Shakespeare lacked sufficient education, aristocratic sensibility, or familiarity with the royal court for a writer of such eminence and genius, scholars reply that there is much <a style=\"text-decoration: underline;\" rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"//www.isnare.com/encyclopedia/Documentary_evidence\" title=\"Documentary evidence\">documentary evidence</a> supporting his authorshipÃ¢Â€Â”title pages, testimony by contemporary poets and historians, official recordsÃ¢Â€Â”and none supporting any other candidate.
